  <script>
   function calcScaleFactor(layoutConfig) {
    let containerSize = layoutConfig.containerW * screen.width / layoutConfig.wideW;
    return containerSize / layoutConfig.containerW;
  }

  function setScaleFactor() {
    let scalingFactor;
    let scalingWidth = 'device-width';
    let orientation = screen.msOrientation || screen.mozOrientation || (screen.orientation || {}).type;
    if ((window.matchMedia("(orientation: portrait)").matches) || window.orientation === 0
      || orientation === "portrait-secondary" || orientation === "portrait-primary") {

      if (screen.width > 768) {
        let layoutConfigPortrait = { containerW: 1024, wideW: 1366 };
        scalingFactor = calcScaleFactor(layoutConfigPortrait);
        scalingFactor = screen.width / layoutConfigPortrait.containerW;
      } else {
        let layoutConfigPortrait = { containerW: 600, wideW: 1024 };
        scalingFactor = calcScaleFactor(layoutConfigPortrait);
      }
      //console.log('## TABLET ## PORTRAIT ---------------------------------------'); 
      //console.log('## TABLET ## PORTRAIT OUTERWIDTH', window.outerWidth);
      console.log('## TABLET ## PORTRAIT =====>', scalingFactor)
      scalingWidth = 1124;
    } else {
      if (screen.width > 1024) {
        let layoutConfigLandscape = { containerW: 1136, wideW: 1440 };
        scalingFactor = calcScaleFactor(layoutConfigLandscape);
      } else {
        let layoutConfigPortrait = { containerW: 1024, wideW: 1136 };
        scalingFactor = calcScaleFactor(layoutConfigPortrait);
        scalingFactor = screen.width / layoutConfigPortrait.containerW;
      }
      //console.log('## TABLET LANDSCAPE ---------------------------------------');
      //console.log('## TABLET ## LANDSCAPE OUTERWIDTH', window.outerWidth);
      console.log('## TABLET ## LANDSCAPE =====>', scalingFactor)
      scalingWidth = 1200;
    }
    if (scalingFactor) {
      console.log('Scale factor [' + scalingFactor + ']');
      Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('meta')).forEach(function (el) {
        if (el.getAttribute('name') === 'viewport') {
          //el.setAttribute('content', 'width=device-width, initial-scale=' + scalingFactor + ', shrink-to-fit=no');
          el.setAttribute('content', 'width=' + scalingWidth + '');
        }
      });
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    //console.log('## TABLET ## ################################################# FIXED ###############################################')
    if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
      setScaleFactor();
    }
  });

  window.addEventListener('orientationchange', function () {
    //console.log('## TABLET ## ################################################# CHANGE ###############################################')
    if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
      setTimeout(() => {
        setScaleFactor();
      }, 100);
    }
  });
  </script>
